(NASDAQ&#58;LULU) today announced financial results for the first quarter of fiscal 2025, which ended on May&#160;4, 2025.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Calvin McDonald, Chief Executive Officer, stated&#58; &#34;In the first quarter, we achieved growth across channels, categories, and markets, including the U.S., reflecting the continued strength and agility of our business model. As we navigate the dynamic macroenvironment, we intend to leverage our strong financial position and competitive advantages to play offense, while we continue to invest in the growth opportunities in front of us.&#34;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">For the first compared to 29.5% for the first quarter of 2024.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;padding-left:22.5pt;text-indent:-22.5pt"><font of 2024.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;padding-left:22.5pt;text-indent:-22.5pt"><font million.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;padding-left:22.5pt;text-indent:-22.5pt"><font We are grateful to our teams around the world who are enabling us to deliver these consistent results.&#34;</font></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Balance Sheet Highlights</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The Company ended the first quarter of 2025 with $1.3 billion in cash and cash equivalents and the capacity under its committed revolving credit facility was $393.4 million.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Inventories at the end of the first quarter of 2025 increased 23% to $1.7 billion compared to $1.3 billion at the end of the first quarter of 2024. On a unit basis, inventories increased 16%.</font></div><div style="height:63pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-top:9pt;text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">1</font></div></div></div><div id="ib56f43452f0c4f8ea70f2dfeae28c5c2_7"></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:99pt;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-top:5pt;text-align:center;text-indent:27pt"><img alt="lululemon_corexlockupxblack.jpg" src="lululemon_corexlockupxblack.jpg" style="height:36px;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:258px"></div></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">2025 Outlook</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">For the second quarter of 2025, the Company expects net revenue to be in the range of $2.535 billion to $2.560 billion, representing growth of 7% to 8%. Diluted earnings per share are expected to be in the range of $2.85 to $2.90 for the quarter. This assumes a tax rate of approximately 30%.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">For 2025, the Company continues to expect net revenue to be in the range of $11.150 billion to $11.300 billion, representing growth of 5% to 7%, or 7% to 8% excluding the 53rd week of 2024. Diluted earnings per share are now expected to be in the range of $14.58 to $14.78 for the year. This assumes a tax rate of approximately 30%.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The guidance does not reflect potential future repurchases of the Company's shares.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The guidance and outlook forward-looking statements made in this press release are based on management's expectations as of the date of this press release and do not incorporate future unknown impacts, including tariffs and macroeconomic trends. The Company undertakes no duty to update or to continue to provide information with respect to any forward-looking statements or risk factors, whether as a result of new information or future events or circumstances or otherwise. Actual results and the timing of events could differ materially from those anticipated in these forward-looking statements as a result of risks and uncertainties, including those stated below.</font></div><div id="ib56f43452f0c4f8ea70f2dfeae28c5c2_13"></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Conference Call Information</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">A conference call to discuss first quarter results is scheduled for today, June&#160;5, 2025, at 4&#58;30 p.m. Eastern time. Those interested in participating in the call are invited to dial 1-833-752-3550 or 1-647-846-8290, if calling internationally, approximately 10 minutes prior to the start of the call. A live webcast of the conference call will be available online at&#58; https&#58;&#47;&#47;corporate.lululemon.com&#47;investors&#47;news-and-events&#47;events-and-presentations. A replay will be made available online approximately two hours following the live call for a period of 30 days.</font></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">About lululemon athletica inc.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">lululemon athletica inc. (NASDAQ&#58;LULU) is a technical athletic apparel, footwear, and accessories company for yoga, running, training, and most other activities, creating transformational products and experiences that build meaningful connections, unlocking greater possibility and wellbeing for all.&#160;Setting the bar in innovation of fabrics and functional designs, lululemon works with yogis and athletes in local communities around the world for continuous research and product feedback.&#160;For more information, visit lululemon.com.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:14pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Shifted Calendar for Comparable Sales</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Due to the 53rd week in 2024, comparable sales are calculated on a one week shifted basis such that the 13 weeks ended May&#160;4, 2025 is compared to the 13 weeks ended May&#160;5, 2024 rather than April&#160;28, 2024.</font></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Non-GAAP Financial Measures</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">We report certain financial metrics on a constant dollar basis, which is a non-GAAP financial measure. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">A constant dollar basis assumes the average foreign currency exchange rates for the period remained constant with the average foreign currency exchange rates for the same period of the prior year. The Company provides constant dollar changes in its results to help investors understand the underlying growth rate of net revenue excluding the impact of changes in foreign currency exchange rates. Management uses constant currency metrics internally when reviewing and assessing financial performance.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The Company's fiscal year ends on the Sunday closest to January&#160;31st of the following year, typically resulting in a 52-week year, but occasionally giving rise to an additional week, resulting in a 53-week year. Fiscal 2024 was a 53-week year while 2025 will be a 52-week year. The expected net revenue increase excluding the 53rd week excludes the net revenue for the </font></div><div style="height:63pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-top:9pt;text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">2</font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:99pt;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-top:5pt;text-align:center;text-indent:27pt"><img alt="lululemon_corexlockupxblack.jpg" src="lululemon_corexlockupxblack.jpg" style="height:36px;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:258px"></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">53rd week of 2024. This enables an evaluation of the expected year-over-year increase in net revenue based on 52 weeks in each year.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">These non-GAAP financial measures are provided in addition to, and not a substitute for, or with greater prominence than, the corresponding financial measures calculated in accordance with GAAP.
